layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda"><a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a></pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

            <a id="3603" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3606" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3606" class="Bound">p₀₁&#39;</a> <a id="3611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3613" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3548" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="3616" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">==</a> <a id="3619" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3577" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="3622" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">[</a> <a id="3624" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3516" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="3626" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="3628" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2113" class="Postulate">p₀₁</a> <a id="3632" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3634" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="3648" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3651" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3651" class="Bound">p₁₀&#39;</a> <a id="3656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3658" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3577" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="3661" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">==</a> <a id="3664" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3548" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="3667" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">[</a> <a id="3669" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3516" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="3671" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="3673" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2133" class="Postulate">p₁₀</a> <a id="3677" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3679" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="3693" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3695" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="3697" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3697" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3699" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3701" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2037" class="Function">pS</a><a id="3703" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3705" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3707" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3516" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="3709" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3697" class="Bound">t</a><a id="3710" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="3724" class="Comment">-------------------------------</a>
            <a id="3768" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3770" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#19996" class="Function">apd</a> <a id="3774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3775" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2885" class="Function">pS-ind</a> <a id="3782" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3516" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="3784" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3548" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="3787" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3577" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="3790" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3606" class="Bound">p₀₁&#39;</a> <a id="3795" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3651" class="Bound">p₁₀&#39;</a><a id="3799" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3801" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2133" class="Postulate">p₁₀</a> <a id="3805" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="3808" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3651" class="Bound">p₁₀&#39;</a></pre>


## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="3980" class="Comment">-- Defs.</a>
<a id="3989" class="Keyword">private</a>
  <a id="p₀₀"></a><a id="3999" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#3999" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="4003" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4005" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="4009" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="4012" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>

              <a id="4081" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>

  <a id="g&#39;"></a><a id="4142" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="4145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4147" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2037" class="Function">pS</a> <a id="4150" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4152" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#940" class="Function">S¹</a>

In the following, we will need the following term:

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4722" class="Comment">-- Homotopy.</a>
  <a id="H₁"></a><a id="4737" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4737" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="4740" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4742" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a> <a id="4745" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4747" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="4750" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#20574" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="4752" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="4757" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4737" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="4760" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4762" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2885" class="Function">pS-ind</a> <a id="4769" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4772" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5577" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="4777" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a><a id="4780" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4782" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4815" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="4785" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4877" class="Function">dpath₀</a> <a id="4792" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#6529" class="Function">dpath₁</a>
    <a id="4803" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="4815" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4815" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="4818" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4820" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a> <a id="4823" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4824" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="4827" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2079" class="Function">pS₁</a><a id="4830" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4832" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="4835" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2079" class="Function">pS₁</a>

      <a id="4877" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4877" class="Function">dpath₀</a> <a id="4884" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="4887" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5577" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="4892" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="4896" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">==</a> <a id="4899" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4815" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="4902" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">[</a> <a id="4904" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="4907" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4907" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="4909" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4911" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4912" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a> <a id="4915" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4917" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a><a id="4919" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4921" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4907" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="4923" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="4926" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a> <a id="4929" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4907" class="Bound">z</a><a id="4930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4932" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="4934" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#2113" class="Postulate">p₀₁</a> <a id="4938" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">]</a>

        <a id="8313" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#8025" class="Function Operator">∎</a></pre>

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8397" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
  <a id="H₂"></a><a id="8411" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8411" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="8414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8416" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="8419" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8421" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a> <a id="8424" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#20574" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="8426" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="8431" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8411" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="8434" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8436" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#1469" class="Function">S¹-ind</a> <a id="8443" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8446" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5577" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8451" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a><a id="8456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8458" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8476" class="Function">q</a>
    <a id="8464" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="8476" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8476" class="Function">q</a> <a id="8478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8480" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5577" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8485" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a> <a id="8491" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">==</a> <a id="8494" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5577" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8499" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a> <a id="8505" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">[</a> <a id="8507" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8510" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8510" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="8512" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8515" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="8518" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8520" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a><a id="8522" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8524" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8510" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="8526" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8529" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a> <a id="8532" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8510" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8533" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8535" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="8537" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#1031" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="8542" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#13131" class="Function">]</a>
      <a id="8550" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8476" class="Function">q</a> <a id="8552" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="8562" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#8085" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
          <a id="8578" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#12006" class="Function">transport</a> <a id="8588" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8591" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8591" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="8593" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8596" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="8599" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8601" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a><a id="8603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8605" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8591" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="8607" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5411" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8610" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a> <a id="8613" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#8591" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8616" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#1031" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="8621" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5465" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

Finally,

### Lemma 2

- Action on paths of pairs

  <a id="11370" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#10389" class="Function">ap-f=pair=</a> <a id="11381" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5465" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="11385" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11385" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="11388" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="11389" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11385" class="DottedPattern Bound">c₁</a> <a id="11392" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5465" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="11396" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11398" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5465" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a></pre>

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11581" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
<a id="neg"></a><a id="11589" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11593" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11595" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3010" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="11600" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11602" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3010" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="11607" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11611" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>  <a id="11617" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11619" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3046" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a>
<a id="11625" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11629" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3046" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a> <a id="11635" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11637" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>

<a id="neg-eq"></a><a id="11643" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11643" class="Function">neg-eq</a> <a id="11650" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11652" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3010" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="11657" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#24413" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="11659" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3010" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="11664" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11643" class="Function">neg-eq</a> <a id="11671" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11673" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#39105" class="Function">qinv-≃</a> <a id="11680" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11685" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11689" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#2268" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11691" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11710" class="Function">h</a> <a id="11693" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#2268" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11695" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11710" class="Function">h</a><a id="11696" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11700" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="11710" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11710" class="Function">h</a> <a id="11712" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11714" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11718" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#4041" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="11720" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11589" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="11724" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#20574" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="11726" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3540" class="Function">id</a>
    <a id="11733" href="2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.html#11710" class="Function">h</a> <a id="11735" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>  <a id="11741" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11743" href="2018-07-06-mini-hott.html#5465" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>
